				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Höchsterwünschtes Freudenfest, BWV 194 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>2 parts (in 12 movements)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1723 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Höchsterwünschtes Freudenfest
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">O greatly longed-for feast of joy
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Authorities
</th>
<td><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.worldcat.org/identities/containsVIAFID/183884682">WorldCat</a>; <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/H%C3%B6chsterw%C3%BCnschtes_Freudenfest,_BWV_194">Wikipedia</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_International_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Virtual International Authority File">VIAF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://viaf.org/viaf/183884682">183884682</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Library_of_Congress_Control_Number" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Library of Congress Control Number">LCCN</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://id.loc.gov/authorities/names/n82162156">n82162156</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Integrated_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Integrated Authority File">GND</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://d-nb.info/gnd/300009011">300009011</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biblioth%C3%A8que_nationale_de_France" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bibliothèque nationale de France">BNF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://catalogue.bnf.fr/ark:/12148/cb139276613">139276613</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Sebastian" title="Category:Bach, Johann Sebastian">Bach, Johann Sebastian</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>BWV 194&#160;; BC A 91a-b&#160;; BC B 31
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 294
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>B-flat major
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>2 parts (in 12 movements):
<dl><dt><ul><li>Prima Parte
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>1. Chorus: Höchsterwünschtes Freudenfest
</dd><dd>2. Recitative (bass): Unendlich großer Gott, ach wende dich
</dd><dd>3. Aria (bass): Was des Höchsten Glanz erfüllt
</dd><dd>4. Recitative (soprano): Wie könnte dir, du höchstes Angesicht
</dd><dd>5. Aria (soprano): Hilf, Gott, dass es uns gelingt
</dd><dd>6. Chorale: Heilger Geist ins Himmels Throne
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>Secondo Parte
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>7. Recitative (tenor): Ihr Heiligen, erfreuet euch
</dd><dd>8. Aria (tenor): Des Höchsten Gegenwart allein
</dd><dd>9. Duet Recitative (soprano, bass): Kann wohl ein Mensch zu Gott im Himmel steigen
</dd><dd>10. Duetto Aria (soprano, bass): O wie wohl ist uns geschehn
</dd><dd>11. Recitative (bass): Wohlan demnach, du heilige Gemeine
</dd><dd>12. Chorale: Sprich Ja zu meinen Taten
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1723 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1723-11-02 in Störmthal (BC B 31, 1st Performance)<br />1724-06-04 in Leipzig (BC A 91a, 2nd Performance)<br />1726-06-16 in Leipzig (BC A 91b, 3rd Performance)<br />1731-05-20 in Leipzig (4th Performance)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1881 (BGA)

<th align="left" style="background-color: #c8dce6">
<ul><li>Cantatas BWV 1–10
</li></ul>
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td style="background-color: #e6f0f5">
<ul><li> BWV 1: <i><a href="/wiki/Wie_sch%C3%B6n_leuchtet_der_Morgenstern,_BWV_1_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Wie schön leuchtet der Morgenstern, BWV 1 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Wie schön leuchtet der Morgenstern</a></i>
</li><li> BWV 2: <i><a href="/wiki/Ach_Gott,_vom_Himmel_sieh_darein,_BWV_2_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Ach Gott, vom Himmel sieh darein, BWV 2 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Ach Gott, vom Himmel sieh darein</a></i>
</li><li> BWV 3: <i><a href="/wiki/Ach_Gott,_wie_manches_Herzeleid,_BWV_3_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Ach Gott, wie manches Herzeleid, BWV 3 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Ach Gott, wie manches Herzeleid</a></i>
</li><li> BWV 4: <i><a href="/wiki/Christ_lag_in_Todes_Banden,_BWV_4_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Christ lag in Todes Banden, BWV 4 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Christ lag in Todes Banden</a></i>
